<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk--hide-tablet stk--hide-mobile stk-block stk-1ca5528 column-spacing" data-v="4" data-block-id="1ca5528"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-1ca5528-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-1ca5528-inner-blocks"></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-5ff099e" data-v="4" data-block-id="5ff099e"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-5ff099e-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-5ff099e-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-13d78e3" id="what-sets-our-preschool-at-marina-boulevard-singapore-apart" data-block-id="13d78e3"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">What Sets our Preschool at Marina Boulevard Singapore Apart</h2></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-3bf6115" data-block-id="3bf6115"><p class="stk-block-text__text">Located in the heart of the CBD, the children at <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Little Skool-House</a> at Marina Boulevard take weekly outdoor walks to learn about iconic landmarks such as the Singapore River and Merlion Park. The centre is also part of the Healthy Meals in Pre-Schools Programme (HMPP) where our <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/our-difference/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">award-winning educators</a> foster a supportive learning environment to educate all our preschoolers about the importance of proper nutrition by providing nutritious meals and promoting an active lifestyle. This ensures parents that our educators will effectively implement the best practices to reap the optimal health and education outcomes.</p></div>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk--hide-tablet stk--hide-mobile stk-block stk-eb0b017 column-spacing" data-v="4" data-block-id="eb0b017"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-eb0b017-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-eb0b017-inner-blocks"></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk--hide-tablet stk--hide-mobile stk-block stk-fd3f91b column-spacing" data-v="4" data-block-id="fd3f91b"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-fd3f91b-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-fd3f91b-inner-blocks"></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk--hide-tablet stk--hide-mobile stk-block stk-19047c3 column-spacing" data-v="4" data-block-id="19047c3"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-19047c3-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-19047c3-inner-blocks"></div></div></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns stk-block-columns stk-block stk-d2878cb" data-animation="fade-in" data-animation-direction="up" data-block-id="d2878cb" style="translate: none; rotate: none; scale: none; transform: translate(0px, 50px); opacity: 0.1;"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-d2878cb-column">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-279c154 masuk-sini" data-v="4" data-block-id="279c154"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-279c154-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-279c154-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns stk-block-columns stk-block stk-75b309c text-block-accordion" data-block-id="75b309c"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-75b309c-column">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-64e0464" data-v="4" data-block-id="64e0464"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-64e0464-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-64e0464-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-f30ae40" id="programmes-offered" data-block-id="f30ae40"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">Programmes Offered</h2></div>



<p>We run full-day programmes for preschoolers that follow either one of two core <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/curriculum/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">curriculums</a> that have been developed specifically for our kindergartens: the <a href="/curriculum/2-months-to-3-years/">relationships-based curriculum</a> and the <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/curriculum/4-to-6-years/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">literacy-based curriculum</a>. This specialised curriculum framework, coupled with Pedagogy for Enhanced Mandarin Acquisition, has led to 93% of Little Skool-House children being <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/our-difference/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Highly Proficient in both English and Mandarin.</a></p>



<p>Your child also has access to our preschool in Raffles Place for a range of <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/curriculum/enrichment-programmes/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">enrichment programmes</a> that address their holistic developmental needs.</p>
</div></div></div>
</div></div>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk--hide-tablet stk--hide-mobile stk-block stk-5a3896f column-spacing" data-v="4" data-block-id="5a3896f"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-5a3896f-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-5a3896f-inner-blocks"></div></div></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-94f2c80 stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="94f2c80"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-94f2c80-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-94f2c80-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-7908c79" data-block-id="7908c79"><p class="stk-block-text__text">At our preschool at Marina Boulevard, Singapore, we offer full-day programmes for preschoolers aged between 18 months and 6 years old. Our educators at the Marina Boulevard follow either one of two core curriculums that has been developed specifically for our kindergartens: the relationships-based curriculum and the literacy-based curriculum. This specialised curriculum framework coupled with Pedagogy for Enhanced Mandarin Acquisition has led to 93% of Little Skool-House children being Highly Proficient in both English and Mandarin.</p></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-subtitle stk-block-subtitle stk-block stk-aeac0bf" data-block-id="aeac0bf"><p class="stk-block-subtitle__text stk-subtitle has-text-color has-text-align-left">Principal</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-subtitle stk-block-subtitle stk-block stk-e74e444" data-block-id="e74e444"><p class="stk-block-subtitle__text stk-subtitle has-text-color has-text-align-left">Bachelor of Science in Early Childhood Education and Leadership Studies (B.SC. in EC)</p></div>
</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-f17e6ac" data-block-id="f17e6ac"><p class="stk-block-text__text">Cindy believes that children need a safe and stimulating environment in order to grow and mature holistically. She encourages children to ask questions, remain curious and engage in critical thinking. She also believes in working closely with parents to ensure continuity in their child’s learning and development at school and at home.</p></div>

</p><p>Governed by ECDA, the Partner Operator (POP) scheme supports appointed centres to improve the accessibility, affordability and quality of childcare and infant care services. Rest assured that our programmes and curriculum are the same across all Little Skool-House centres.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Within the Little Skool-House network of centres, 14 of them operate as Partner Operator (POP) centres under the Partner Operator scheme governed by ECDA. This programme aims to improve accessibility, affordability and quality of childcare and infant care services for working parents. 12 of these centres operate on the premises of our partner employer. However, in all other aspects, our POP centres are consistent with all other Little Skool-House centres in the delivery of programmes and curriculum.</p>
